WIRING REGULATIONS

WIRING COLORS
Main current AC black (BK) Control circuit AC > 50V red (RD) after Control transformer External voltage orange (OG)
Main current DC black (BK) Control circuit AC < 50V red (RD) after Control transformer Interlock circuit orange (OG)
Neutral conductor blue (BU) Control circuit 24Vdc dark blue (DBU) Measuring lines white (WH)
Protective wire green-yellow (GNYE) Control circuit GND dark blue/white (DBU/WH)
MINIMUM CROSS-SECTIONS WIRING
Main current 1,5 mm² 0.5 - 1.0 mm² H05V-K PVC conductor line
